    - 1/2 cup peanut butter or almond butter

    - 1/3 cup honey or maple syrup
    - 1 tsp vanilla extract

    Instructions:

    6. Store the energy balls in an airtight container in the refrigerator for up to a week.

  • Test (2024-06-04 04:42:23.020980): I am pretty snacky for some sweet treats.
  • Agent (2024-06-04 04:42:25.688226): I'm here to help! How about trying a delicious homemade chocolate chip cookie recipe? Here's a simple one for you:

    Ingredients:
    - 1 cup unsalted butter ( melted )
    - 1 cup white sugar
    - 1 cup packed brown sugar
    - 2 eggs
    - 2 teaspoons vanilla extract
    - 3 cups all-purpose flour
    - 1 teaspoon baking soda
    - 1/2 teaspoon salt
    - 2 cups chocolate chips
    - 1 cup chopped nuts (optional)

    Instructions:
    1. Preheat your oven to 375°F (190°C).
    2. In a large bowl, mix together the melted butter, white sugar, and brown sugar until smooth.
    3. Beat in the eggs one at a time, then stir in the vanilla extract.
    4. In a separate bowl, combine the flour, baking soda, and salt. Gradually mix this into the sugar mixture.
    5. Fold in the chocolate chips and nuts (if using).
    6. Drop by large spoonfuls onto ungreased baking sheets.
    7. Bake for about 10 minutes in the preheated oven, or until edges are nicely browned. Enjoy your homemade chocolate chip cookies!

    Please note that if you have any dietary restrictions or allergies, feel free to modify this recipe to suit your needs. For example, use gluten-free flour, vegan butter, and dairy-free chocolate chips to make it gluten-free and vegan.

  • Test (2024-06-04 08:56:35.238299): I am pretty snacky for some sweet treats.

    Ingredients:
    - 1 cup rolled oats
    - 2/3 cup toasted coconut flakes
    - 1/2 cup peanut butter or almond butter
    - 1/2 cup ground flaxseed
    - 1/2 cup chocolate chips (or dried fruit for a healthier alternative)
    - 1/3 cup honey or maple syrup
    - 1 tsp vanilla extract

    Instructions:
    1. Mix all the dry ingredients (oats, coconut flakes, flaxseed, and chocolate chips) in a large bowl.
    2. In a separate bowl, combine the peanut butter, honey, and vanilla extract.
    3. Pour the wet mixture into the dry mixture and stir until well combined.
    4. Let the mixture chill in the refrigerator for about 30 minutes.
    5. Roll the chilled mixture into bite-sized balls.
    6. Store the energy balls in an airtight container in the refrigerator for up to a week.

    These energy balls make a perfect sweet treat without any added processed sugars. The oats, flaxseed, and nut butters provide fiber, protein, and healthy fats, while the chocolate chips or dried fruit add a touch of natural sweetness. Enjoy your snack!
